# Query 4: 73.46 QPS, 0.09x concurrency, ID 0xA2207B1E5D48A65E366B2D481D2D9508 at byte 3571127
# This item is included in the report because it matches --limit.
# Scores: V/M = 0.07
# Time range: 2023-11-05T10:55:54 to 2023-11-05T10:56:55

# Count          2    4481
# Exec time      8      6s   104us   206ms     1ms   490us    10ms   159us
# Lock time      3     8ms       0   336us     1us     1us     5us     1us
# Rows sent      1   4.38k       1       1       1       1       0       1
# Rows examine   0   4.38k       1       1       1       1       0       1

# Tables
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'posts'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`posts`\G
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'users'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`users`\G
# EXPLAIN /*!50100 PARTITIONS*/
SELECT
		posts.id AS post_id,
		posts.user_id AS post_user_id,
		posts.body AS post_body,
		posts.mime AS post_mime,
		posts.created_at AS post_created_at,
		users.account_name AS user_account_name,
		users.passhash AS user_passhash,
		users.authority AS user_authority,
		users.del_flg AS user_del_flg,
		users.created_at AS user_created_at
	FROM posts JOIN users
	ON users.id = posts.user_id
	WHERE posts.id = 2624
	ORDER BY posts.created_at DESC
	LIMIT 20\G

# Query 6: 17.18 QPS, 0.05x concurrency, ID 0x167A66FDC6782564234F598BDD504CEB at byte 5355125
# This item is included in the report because it matches --limit.
# Scores: V/M = 0.16
# Time range: 2023-11-05T10:55:54 to 2023-11-05T10:56:55
# Attribute    pct   total     min     max     avg     95%  stddev  median
# ============ === ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= =======
# Count          0    1048
# Exec time      4      3s   155us   410ms     3ms     1ms    21ms   260us
# Lock time      0     2ms       0   121us     1us     1us     3us     1us
# Rows sent      4  10.46k       2      20   10.22   14.52    2.90    9.83
# Rows examine   1  10.46k       2      20   10.22   14.52    2.90    9.83
# Query size     0 537.21k     524     525  524.91  511.45       0  511.45
# String:
# Databases    isuconp
# Hosts        localhost
# Users        isuconp
# Query_time distribution
#   1us
#  10us
# 100us  ################################################################
#   1ms  ##
#  10ms  #
# 100ms  #
#    1s
#  10s+
# Tables
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'posts'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`posts`\G
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'users'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`users`\G
# EXPLAIN /*!50100 PARTITIONS*/
SELECT
		posts.id AS post_id,
		posts.user_id AS post_user_id,
		posts.body AS post_body,
		posts.mime AS post_mime,
		posts.created_at AS post_created_at,
		users.account_name AS user_account_name,
		users.passhash AS user_passhash,
		users.authority AS user_authority,
		users.del_flg AS user_del_flg,
		users.created_at AS user_created_at
	FROM posts FORCE INDEX (user_id_created_at_index)
	JOIN users
	ON users.id = posts.user_id
	WHERE users.del_flg = 0
	AND posts.user_id = 83
	ORDER BY posts.created_at DESC
	LIMIT 20\G

# Query 9: 29.83 QPS, 0.03x concurrency, ID 0x13E1CA57A12AF0BA1E6562A566821C3A at byte 7630805
# This item is included in the report because it matches --limit.
# Scores: V/M = 0.04
# Time range: 2023-11-05T10:55:55 to 2023-11-05T10:56:55
# Attribute    pct   total     min     max     avg     95%  stddev  median
# ============ === ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= ======= =======
# Count          1    1790
# Exec time      2      2s   258us   164ms   867us   881us     6ms   403us
# Lock time      1     3ms     1us    83us     1us     1us     2us     1us
# Rows sent     14  34.96k      20      20      20      20       0      20
# Rows examine  12  71.91k      40      44   41.14   42.48    1.21   40.45
# Query size     0 952.69k     545     545     545     545       0     545
# String:
# Databases    isuconp
# Hosts        localhost
# Users        isuconp
# Query_time distribution
#   1us
#  10us
# 100us  ################################################################
#   1ms  ##
#  10ms  #
# 100ms  #
#    1s
#  10s+
# Tables
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'posts'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`posts`\G
#    SHOW TABLE STATUS FROM `isuconp` LIKE 'users'\G
#    SHOW CREATE TABLE `isuconp`.`users`\G
# EXPLAIN /*!50100 PARTITIONS*/
SELECT
		posts.id AS post_id,
		posts.user_id AS post_user_id,
		posts.body AS post_body,
		posts.mime AS post_mime,
		posts.created_at AS post_created_at,
		users.account_name AS user_account_name,
		users.passhash AS user_passhash,
		users.authority AS user_authority,
		users.del_flg AS user_del_flg,
		users.created_at AS user_created_at
	FROM posts FORCE INDEX (created_at_index)
	JOIN users
	ON users.id = posts.user_id
	WHERE users.del_flg = 0
	AND posts.created_at <= '2016-01-02T11:45:28+09:00'
	ORDER BY posts.created_at DESC
	LIMIT 20\G
